\nComponent 'redaction_prompt':\nGiven a private user query, create a privacy-preserving request for a powerful external LLM. The LLM may assist without learning private information about the user.  

**Key Requirements:**  
1. **Remove all personally identifiable information (PII):**  
   - Omit names (e.g., "Ms. Amanda," "fxu80pep"), specific locations (e.g., "Madera," "/home/fxu80pep/public_html/pro_login.php"), technical details (e.g., server names, database schemas), and any other data that could uniquely identify the user or their context.  
   - Replace sensitive terms (e.g., "ariel," "root," "VIMS (France)") with generic placeholders (e.g., "hostname," "user," "brand") unless the query explicitly requires retention for clarity (e.g., "United Arab Republic").  

2. **Preserve core intent and structure:**  
   - Retain the original query's purpose, key facts, and required outcomes (e.g., troubleshooting steps, document structure, historical analysis).  
   - Use placeholders for non-essential details (e.g., "X" for numbers, "YYYY" for years, "Company A" for organizations) when removing specific data would obscure the query's purpose.  

3. **Output only the redacted request:**  
   - Do not include explanations, reasoning, or conversational filler. The output must be a standalone, actionable query for the LLM.  

**Examples of PII to Redact:**  
- Names (e.g., "Ms. Amanda," "Your Name")  
- File paths, URLs, or technical specifications (e.g., "/home/fxu80pep/public_html/pro_login.php," "postgresql://ariel:5432/Anostic")  
- Sensitive credentials (e.g., "root," "passwords")  
- Specific organizations or brands (e.g., "VIMS (France)," "Hermann (Germany)") unless required for context.  

**Generalizable Strategy:**  
- Strip all unique identifiers, anonymize entities, and retain only the functional components of the query. Ensure the redacted request is clear, concise, and actionable for the LLM to assist without learning private details.
\nComponent 'response_prompt':\nRespond to a user query. For inspiration, we found a potentially related request to a powerful external LLM and its response.

Input:
1. related_llm_request: The privacy-preserving request sent to the external LLM.
2. related_llm_response: Information from a powerful LLM responding to the related request.
3. user_query: The user's original request you need to fulfill.

Instruction: Generate your final response to the user's request. Output ONLY the response.
